<div id="review_249982778" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/249982778" />
    <a title="shady boots" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4972138-shady-boots"><img alt="shady boots" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1592459241p2/4972138.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/249982778?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="shady boots" class="user" itemprop="url" name="shady boots" href="/user/show/4972138-shady-boots">shady boots</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=covergasm">covergasm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=all-time-faves">all-time-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=2012-faves">2012-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=heroines-i-adore">heroines-i-adore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=oh-my-god-marry-me">oh-my-god-marry-me</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer249982778" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2982423647159338704">This review is also available over at <a href='http://wildheartbookblogs.blogspot.com/2012/10/review-burn-for-burn-by-jenny-han.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>my blog.</a><br/><br/>_____________________<br/><br/>Actual rating is <b>4.5</b> stars.<br/><br/>I cannot even tell you how excited I was to read this book. The beautiful cover and the badass blurb was way too hard to resist. I can safely say that this book didn't disappoint me at all. I ended up reading it so fast because it just pulled me in that much. But I have to take away half a star due to a tiny little detail that I'll explain later in this review.<br/><br/>So the book is told from the POVs of Mary, </span>
  <span id="freeText2982423647159338704" style="display:none">This review is also available over at <a href="http://wildheartbookblogs.blogspot.com/2012/10/review-burn-for-burn-by-jenny-han.html" rel="nofollow noopener">my blog.</a><br /><br />_____________________<br /><br />Actual rating is <b>4.5</b> stars.<br /><br />I cannot even tell you how excited I was to read this book. The beautiful cover and the badass blurb was way too hard to resist. I can safely say that this book didn't disappoint me at all. I ended up reading it so fast because it just pulled me in that much. But I have to take away half a star due to a tiny little detail that I'll explain later in this review.<br /><br />So the book is told from the POVs of Mary, Lillia and Kat. Mary is a girl who had left Jar Island because of a boy, who tormented her and hurt her badly, but now she's coming back to prove to him that she isn't the same girl anymore. Lillia is beautiful and popular, but this summer a boy went way too far, and she'll do whatever it takes to protect her little sister Nadia and not let the same thing happen to her. Kat is sick and tired of all the ridicule she's been getting in her school, and the only one to blame for it all is her ex-best friend Rennie, the school's most popular girl, and Kat is ready to make her pay. Three very different girls who unite from wanting the same thing: revenge.<br /><br />I loved all three of the girls. I thought their voices were very distinct, and they never meshed together. Mary was a little meh during the first few chapters, but I grew to like her more eventually. Lillia was also a very likable character, and I actually liked her overprotective-ness over her little sister. Kat was awesome and badass, and she was I guess the glue that kept the three girls together. The mastermind, if you will.<br /><br />There wasn't really a romance in this book. Kat had this thing going on with one of the guys in the book, but it was pretty complicated. And it also seemed like that same guy wanted to be with Lillia. As far as Mary goes, she had feelings for the guy who tormented her, despite everything he did. I felt bad for her, and I kind of want her to get a love interest of her own so she doesn't seem so sad all the time. But the romance was the last thing I cared about or paid attention to when reading the book.<br /><br />Okay, I need to address the whole supernatural thing. It was <i>extremely</i> subtle. Like, it was barely even there until near the end, when everything pretty much blows out of proportion. And it also seemed to be tied to just one girl in particular, not all three of them. It really confused me. If I used percentages, I would say this book is 98% contemporary and 2% supernatural. I do hope it gets addressed more in the sequel, though, cause I really am confused.<br /><br />The ending, as I just mentioned, was insane. Everything just explodes─<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and I may mean that in a literal sense <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>─and it ended so abruptly. It was a very massive cliffhanger indeed, and I've no doubt it'll make the wait for book two extremely painful.<br /><br />Overall this was a very very good book. I pretty much liked everything about it. I had to take away half due to the confusing and slightly too subtle supernatural aspect, but I'm definitely excited to see where this series will go in the future.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_2021558663" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Mel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10697179-mel"><img alt="Mel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580549097p2/10697179.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mel" href="/user/show/10697179-mel">Mel</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781442440760" href="/book/show/17334509-burn-for-burn">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10697179-mel?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10697179-mel?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2021558663" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8268204593742207240">I'd say 4.5 stars, just because it did have a lot of flaws, but I really really enjoyed this book.<br/><br/>I read the entire thing in under 24 hours, and loved every second. I was thoroughly immersed in the writing, the characters, the setting, and the revenge story. I haven't read a book this quickly in a long time and it was a ton of fun.<br/><br/>I really only had 2 little qualms about it. I did not like the weird Carrie-like twist at the end. It makes me worry about the next 2 books and whether they will hold </span>
  <span id="freeText8268204593742207240" style="display:none">I'd say 4.5 stars, just because it did have a lot of flaws, but I really really enjoyed this book.<br /><br />I read the entire thing in under 24 hours, and loved every second. I was thoroughly immersed in the writing, the characters, the setting, and the revenge story. I haven't read a book this quickly in a long time and it was a ton of fun.<br /><br />I really only had 2 little qualms about it. I did not like the weird Carrie-like twist at the end. It makes me worry about the next 2 books and whether they will hold the same enjoyment this one did since what I liked about it was the contemporary aspect of it.<br /><br />I also didn't like how sexual assault is really just brushed aside in this. There was an instance of sexual assault in the book, well we got to hear that it happened, but I didn't like how the character seemingly "got over it" and the effects basically stopped being talked about after the one day, and once we got the full story, it was really never brought up or talked about again. It's not underplayed in the slightest, and it wasn't shied about, but it just seemed like the character got over it and it felt weird that it never came up again.<br /><br />Otherwise I just devoured this book and really ended up enjoying the entire thing. I cannot wait to continue the series and see where it goes, despite my worry about the Carrie thing.</span>

<div id="review_152626693" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/152626693" />
    <a title="Jasprit" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4841793-jasprit"><img alt="Jasprit" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1456315622p2/4841793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/152626693?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasprit" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasprit" href="/user/show/4841793-jasprit">Jasprit</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4841793-jasprit?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4841793-jasprit?shelf=out-2012">out-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4841793-jasprit?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4841793-jasprit?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4841793-jasprit?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer152626693" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13155755803932925019">Being a huge fan of Jenny Han’s books, when I first heard about Burn for Burn, I knew I had to get my hands on a copy. Also Siobhan Vivian was an author whose books I had been promising myself to getting around to for ages. So I knew picking up this book would be a win-win situation!<br/><br/>Burn for Burn focuses on three girls, Kat, Mary and Lillia forced to work together on one common goal; revenge. You know the saying revenge is a dish best served cold? Well this saying totally applied here. The three</span>
  <span id="freeText13155755803932925019" style="display:none">Being a huge fan of Jenny Han’s books, when I first heard about Burn for Burn, I knew I had to get my hands on a copy. Also Siobhan Vivian was an author whose books I had been promising myself to getting around to for ages. So I knew picking up this book would be a win-win situation!<br /><br />Burn for Burn focuses on three girls, Kat, Mary and Lillia forced to work together on one common goal; revenge. You know the saying revenge is a dish best served cold? Well this saying totally applied here. The three girls had their own reasons for getting their own back on Reeve, Alex and Rennie. Whereas Kat and Lillia used to be close friends until Rennie ruined it, Mary’s the school newbie. But the three girls manage to form a united alliance, with devious plans up their sleeves, they’re sure to get their comeuppance.<br /><br />Burn for Burn lets us into the story through povs from Mary, Kat and Lillia. As I read through the chapters I really felt I got to know Kat and Lillia, the hardships they had to experience, the pressure they had to deal with and keeping their mouth shut when necessary. But with Mary, I don’t know, I liked getting her back story, how she had a tough time and how much it took to get to where she is now. But there were aspects concerning her which I just didn’t get; her super creepy aunt, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ her so called powers  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I think it was purposely done this way to just scratch the surface with Mary’s character, but I think I wanted more from her.<br /><br />The so-called revenge plan I was totally on board with, I agreed that all three deserved their just deserts especially Rennie, ugh I couldn’t stand this girl! And by the end of the book my opinion didn’t change of her, but Alex really grew on me as the as the book progressed, I began to feel really sorry for him and hoped the girls would stop their revenge act towards him. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ but the thing that confused me with him, he wasn’t really clear about his feelings towards Lillia or Kat, for the majority of the book I got the expression that he liked Lillia, but then one part at the dance I thought he liked Kat, I know some readers may not really be bothered by this, but I really needed to know about his true feelings.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Also Reeve being the obnoxious boy that he was really messed around with my feelings at the end <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the drugs seemed to bring out the real boy underneath, and he seemed so lonely and lost and I just wanted to give him a big hug!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />Overall Burn for Burn was an exceptional first book to a fresh new series. I really feel as if I know Kat and Lillia so well already and so I can’t wait to see which direction book two Fire with Fire will take us to next!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13155755803932925019" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review152626693">
  <td colspan="2">

<div id="review_602117661" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/602117661" />
    <a title="Jamie-leigh Haughn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17182207-jamie-leigh-haughn"><img alt="Jamie-leigh Haughn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483227714p2/17182207.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/602117661?book_show_action=true">Apr 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie-leigh Haughn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie-leigh Haughn" href="/user/show/17182207-jamie-leigh-haughn">Jamie-leigh Haughn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17182207-jamie-leigh-haughn?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer602117661" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2683982075779301798">OH MY GOD<br/><br/>I went in to this book expecting it to be just a light fun contemporary.... but boy was I wrong! This book had me completely engulfed after the first few chapters. I loved having the perspectives of the three girls, Kat, Lillia and Mary. Each girl is so different and had really interesting reasons on why they wanted revenge, yet they all kind of intertwined. I think of the three girls I liked Mary the best, although its really hard to choose, they are pretty equal, I definitely enjoyed </span>
  <span id="freeText2683982075779301798" style="display:none">OH MY GOD<br /><br />I went in to this book expecting it to be just a light fun contemporary.... but boy was I wrong! This book had me completely engulfed after the first few chapters. I loved having the perspectives of the three girls, Kat, Lillia and Mary. Each girl is so different and had really interesting reasons on why they wanted revenge, yet they all kind of intertwined. I think of the three girls I liked Mary the best, although its really hard to choose, they are pretty equal, I definitely enjoyed Mary's back story the best. I also liked how while reading this book at times I really wanted Reeve, Alex and Rennie to get screwed over but then it would show something that made you feel for them. I really liked Alex and then all of a sudden I hated him... then I liked him again. I loved how it played with your emotions and your head!<br /><br />This book reminded me a lot of John Tucker must die, only with many different levels. It was really well crafted in the fact that I just couldn't put this book down. The ending left me wanting more, I need the second book NOW!!!<br /><br />Loved it! A great revenge story, I for sure recommend it!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="2683982075779301798" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PPE+XpEmPW6ZLIQsXBzPFx1MmVwUXaAvN3O27lBnk2mwd3wHaiCtX3saTCEwhKP2CKPnAPtmINLiplZV+NoLaw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ykP6hH5jI6mBxw9+piFcGtPmtKXbnkU3vi3DHzIP65lGxbjdhWWzmGPxx3PKuTD7xgnK+TSlxcpr+COkmrJzmw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
